Management Zone API documentation version v1

http://api.management-zone.syngenta.com/api/v1/management-zone

/filter

/filter post

post

API will return geometry assets based on geojson geometry and filter parameter.

post /filter

API will return geometry assets based on geojson geometry and filter parameter.

  • Request
  • Response

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • field_id: (string)

    farm Field Id

  • geojson: required(object)

    Geojson including coordinates

    • type: required(string)
    • features: required(array of Type.Feature)

      Items: Feature

      • type: required(string)
      • properties: required(object)
      • geometry: required(object)
        • type: required(string)
        • coordinates: required(array of array)
  • filter: required(object)

    Filters with start date and source

    • fromDate: required(date-only)

      start date(yyyy-mm-dd)

    • sources: required(array of string)

      list of source names

Example:

{
   "field_id":"5cf7675a-7be7-453f-b66b-5f6b0a4c857f",
   "geojson":{
      "type":"FeatureCollection",
      "features":[
         {
            "type":"Feature",
            "properties":{

            },
            "geometry":{
               "type":"Polygon",
               "coordinates":[
                  [
                     [
                        -76.64285659790039,
                        35.1770355550041
                     ],
                     [
                        -76.6157341003418,
                        35.1770355550041
                     ],
                     [
                        -76.6157341003418,
                        35.194151800350454
                     ],
                     [
                        -76.64285659790039,
                        35.194151800350454
                     ],
                     [
                        -76.64285659790039,
                        35.1770355550041
                     ]
                  ]
               ]
            }
         }
      ]
   },
   "filter":
   {
     "fromDate": "2001-04-01",
     "sources":[
       "Drone",
       "sentinal"
     ]
 }
}

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • geom_id: required(string)
  • assets: required(array of Type.Asset)

    Items: Asset

    • asset_id: required(string)
    • cloud_cover: required(number)
    • acquisition_date: required(datetime)
    • source: required(string)

Example:

{
  "geom_id":"625b8d77-50f6-46d8-9736-c513fef863d2",
  "assets":[
   {
      "asset_id":"LC08_L1GT_014035_20191008_20191009_01_RT",
      "cloud_cover":0.9995999999999999,
      "acquisition_date":"2019-10-08T15:41:26Z",
      "source":"landsat8"
   },
   {
      "asset_id":"LC08_L1GT_014035_20200112_20200112_01_RT",
      "cloud_cover":0.9998,
      "acquisition_date":"2020-01-12T15:41:15Z",
      "source":"landsat8"
   },
   {
      "asset_id":"LC08_L1GT_014035_20200401_20200401_01_RT",
      "cloud_cover":0.9992,
      "acquisition_date":"2020-04-01T15:40:45Z",
      "source":"landsat8"
   }
]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • items: required(array of Type.Error)

    Items: Error

    • severity: required(one of warn, error, info)
    • code: required(string)

      error code

    • message: required(string)

      message

    • field: required(string)

Example:

{
  "items":[
    {
      "severity":"error",
      "code":"required",
      "field":"field_id",
      "message":"field_id is required"
    },
    {
      "severity":"error",
      "code":"required",
      "field":"asset_id",
      "message":"asset_id is required"
    }
  ]
}

    Items: Feature
